delequip EQI_ARMOR;
if (.@gamble < 81){
getitem 2792,1;
if (achievementexists(240071) == 0){
achievementcomplete(240071);
}
mes "[Mash The Blacksmith]";
mes "It has been done.";
}
else {
mes "[Mash The Blacksmith]";
mes "Oh, no...";
next;
mes "[Mash The Blacksmith]";
mes "The ritual has failed.";
next;
mes "[Mash The Blacksmith]";
mes "I'm so sorry...";
}
}
else {
mes "[Mash The Blacksmith]";
mes "You have got to be kidding me.";
}
}
else {
mes "[Mash The Blacksmith]";
mes "You have got to be kidding me.";
}
close;
end;

tht2s:
next;
mes "[Mash The Blacksmith]";
mes "Before we continue, you must be wearing the +10 Tights [1] that you want to Upgrade.";
mes "^FF0000(WARNING: ALL CARDS COMPOUNDED INTO THE ARMOR WILL BE LOST)^000000";
mes "^FF0000(THERE IS A 20% CHANCE THE PROCESS WILL FAIL)^000000";
menu "Let's do it.",tht2sgo;

tht2sgo:
next;
if (getequipid(EQI_ARMOR) == 2331){
if (getequiprefinerycnt(EQI_ARMOR) == 10 && countitem(6940) > 999 && countitem(20089) > 0){
set .@gamble,rand(1,100);
delitem 6940,1000;
delitem 20089,1;
delequip EQI_ARMOR;
if (.@gamble < 81){
getitem 2363,1;
if (achievementexists(240071) == 0){

}

mes "It has been done.";
}
else {

next;

mes "The ritual has failed.";
next;
mes "[Mash The Blacksmith]";
mes "I'm so sorry...";
}
}
else {
mes "[Mash The Blacksmith]";
mes "You have got to be kidding me.";
}
}
else {
mes "[Mash The Blacksmith]";
mes "You have got to be kidding me.";
}
close;
end;
